   Answer: a

2339. EFFECT :

   c) the hot sun always has a burning effect on my skin
   d) the production relied too much on spectacular effects

   Answer: a

   c) the committee said that they feel like an advice bureau
   d) he was too proud to ever seek advice

2341. CROP :

   d) we had a bumper crop this year

   c) what do they charge for room and boarding? (ANSWER - *The error is that the noun 'BOARD' is typically used for the body of people, or the wooden plank; 'boarding' is the noun for the meal/lodging service.*)
   d) dinner will be served on board the plane.

   Answer: a

4160. EFFECT :
   a) impatient investors effected our roll out date (ANSWER - *The verb 'affected' (influenced) would be the more appropriate word, making 'effected' (brought about) the less appropriate usage here.*)

   c) the hot sun always has a burning effect on my skin
   d) the production relied too much on spectacular effects

   Answer: a

   c) the committee said that they feel like an advice bureau
   d) he was too proud to ever seek advice

   Answer: a

   d) we had a bumper crop this year

   Answer: a
